Model:     I understand the problem better now. The key issue is that all `move_base` actions must be exactly as provided in the list of valid actions. My previous interpretation of using `#o3` as an intermediate universal configuration was incorrect, as the specific transition actions themselves (`move_base <from> #o3 #o0` or `move_base #o3 <to> #o0`) were not allowed as a general pattern, but only the exact ones listed. The valid `move_base` actions are very limited and specific.
           
           Given the initial state `atbconf(v3)`, the only valid `move_base` action from `v3` is `(move_base v3 #o3 #o0)`. This means the robot must first move to `#o3`. All other `move_base` actions *start* from `#o3` or end *at* `#o3`. This means `#o3` is the main "hub" for all base movements.
           
           So, the new revised strategy for each object is:
           1. Move from current base config (initially `v3`, later the base config after `place`) to `#o3`.
           2. Move from `#o3` to the pick config.
           3. Perform the `pick` action.
           4. Move from the pick config to `#o3`.
           5. Move from `#o3` to the place config.
           6. Perform the `place` action.
           
           Let's trace this path for each object, making sure every `move_base`, `pick`, and `place` action is *exactly* from the provided valid action list.
